```python
"""
Artifact and task_card lifecycle transitions enforced at runtime (lifecycle gate).

For agents: illegal transitions raise ContractValidationError with LIFECYCLE_VIOLATION.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

from typing import TYPE_CHECKING

from .contracts import ArtifactStatus, TaskCardStatus
from .errors import ContractErrorDetail, ContractValidationError

if TYPE_CHECKING:
    pass

_TASK_CARD_TRANSITIONS: dict[TaskCardStatus, frozenset[TaskCardStatus]] = {
    TaskCardStatus.PENDING: frozenset(
        {TaskCardStatus.RUNNING, TaskCardStatus.CANCELLED},
    ),
    TaskCardStatus.RUNNING: frozenset(
        {
            TaskCardStatus.BLOCKED,
            TaskCardStatus.COMPLETED,
            TaskCardStatus.FAILED,
            TaskCardStatus.CANCELLED,
        },
    ),
    TaskCardStatus.BLOCKED: frozenset(
        {TaskCardStatus.RUNNING, TaskCardStatus.CANCELLED, TaskCardStatus.FAILED},
    ),
    TaskCardStatus.COMPLETED: frozenset(),
    TaskCardStatus.FAILED: frozenset(),
    TaskCardStatus.CANCELLED: frozenset(),
}

_ARTIFACT_TRANSITIONS: dict[ArtifactStatus, frozenset[ArtifactStatus]] = {
    ArtifactStatus.ACTIVE: frozenset(
        {
            ArtifactStatus.SUPERSEDED,
            ArtifactStatus.INVALIDATED,
            ArtifactStatus.ARCHIVED,
        },
    ),
    ArtifactStatus.SUPERSEDED: frozenset({ArtifactStatus.ARCHIVED}),
    ArtifactStatus.INVALIDATED: frozenset({ArtifactStatus.ARCHIVED}),
    ArtifactStatus.ARCHIVED: frozenset(),
}


def assert_task_card_transition(
    *,
    from_status: TaskCardStatus,
    to_status: TaskCardStatus,
    schema_id: str = "https://xlotyl.local/schemas/control-plane/v1/task-card.schema.json",
) -> None:
    allowed = _TASK_CARD_TRANSITIONS.get(from_status, frozenset())
    if to_status not in allowed:
        raise ContractValidationError(
            error_code="LIFECYCLE_VIOLATION",
            contract_type="TASK_CARD",
            schema_id=schema_id,
            details=[
                ContractErrorDetail(
                    path="/status",
                    message=f"Illegal transition {from_status!s} -> {to_status!s}",
                    keyword="lifecycle",
                )
            ],
        )


def assert_artifact_transition(
    *,
    from_status: ArtifactStatus,
    to_status: ArtifactStatus,
    schema_id: str = "https://xlotyl.local/schemas/control-plane/v1/artifact-record.schema.json",
) -> None:
    allowed = _ARTIFACT_TRANSITIONS.get(from_status, frozenset())
    if to_status not in allowed:
        raise ContractValidationError(
            error_code="LIFECYCLE_VIOLATION",
            contract_type="ARTIFACT_RECORD",
            schema_id=schema_id,
            details=[
                ContractErrorDetail(
                    path="/status",
                    message=f"Illegal transition {from_status!s} -> {to_status!s}",
                    keyword="lifecycle",
                )
            ],
        )
```

### `services/response-control-framework/src/response_control_framework/response_control.py`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 21334 bytes

```python
"""Three-choice / five-layer response-control evaluation.

The control plane owns the independent choices:
agent profile (x), domain knowledge package (y), and runtime environment (z).
Technique (z1) is derived from selected runtime environments, and theory (y1)
is derived from selected domain knowledge packages.

Rich policy prose in ``knowledge/response-control/*.json`` (compiled from the wiki)
is authoritative for *selection* here; injecting full policy text into LLM prompts
is a separate gateway/agent concern—callers that need prose should map
``selected_agent_profile`` (and related refs) to catalog fields explicitly.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import re
from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import UTC, datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from uuid import NAMESPACE_URL, uuid5

from .contracts import (
    DomainKnowledgePackagePayload,
    AgentProfileDissonance,
    AgentProfileSelection,
    RuntimeEnvironmentPayload,
    RuntimeEnvironmentKind,
    RuntimeEnvironmentSelection,
    ResponseControlAssessment,
    AgentProfileKey,
    AgentProfilePayload,
    TechniqueCardPayload,
    TechniqueSelection,
    TheoryCardPayload,
    DomainKnowledgePackageSelection,
)

ASSEMBLY_ORDER = [
    "agent_profile",
    "domain_knowledge_package",
    "runtime_environment",
    "technique",
    "theory",
]

_AGENT_PROFILE_ALIASES = {
    "strict": AgentProfileKey.ENGINEERING,
    "strict_engineering": AgentProfileKey.ENGINEERING,
    "engineering_task": AgentProfileKey.ENGINEERING,
    "definition": AgentProfileKey.DICTIONARY_DEFINITION,
    "dictionary": AgentProfileKey.DICTIONARY_DEFINITION,
    "dictionary/definition": AgentProfileKey.DICTIONARY_DEFINITION,
    "direct_query": AgentProfileKey.QUERY,
    "qa": AgentProfileKey.QUERY,
}


@dataclass(frozen=True)
class ResponseControlCatalog:
    agent_profiles: dict[str, AgentProfilePayload]
    domain_knowledge_packages: dict[str, DomainKnowledgePackagePayload]
    runtime_environments: dict[str, RuntimeEnvironmentPayload]
    techniques: dict[str, TechniqueCardPayload]
    theory: dict[str, TheoryCardPayload]

    @classmethod
    def load(cls, root: Path | None = None) -> ResponseControlCatalog:
        base = root or _catalog_root()
        return cls(
            agent_profiles={
                item.agent_profile_id: item
                for item in _load_cards(base / "agent-profiles.json", AgentProfilePayload)
            },
            domain_knowledge_packages={
                item.domain_knowledge_package_id: item
                for item in _load_cards(
                    base / "domain-knowledge-packages.json", DomainKnowledgePackagePayload
                )
            },
            runtime_environments={
                item.runtime_environment_id: item
                for item in _load_cards(base / "runtime-environments.json", RuntimeEnvironmentPayload)
            },
            techniques={
                item.technique_card_id: item
                for item in _load_cards(base / "techniques.json", TechniqueCardPayload)
            },
            theory={
                item.theory_card_id: item
                for item in _load_cards(base / "theory.json", TheoryCardPayload)
            },
        )


_CATALOG_CACHE: tuple[str, ResponseControlCatalog] | None = None


def reset_response_control_catalog_cache_for_tests() -> None:
    global _CATALOG_CACHE  # noqa: PLW0603 - intentional process-local cache
    _CATALOG_CACHE = None


def response_control_artifact_ref(
    assessment: ResponseControlAssessment | dict[str, Any],
) -> str:
    identifier = (
        assessment.response_control_assessment_id
        if isinstance(assessment, ResponseControlAssessment)
        else assessment["response_control_assessment_id"]
    )
    return f"artifact://response-control-assessment/{identifier}"


def selected_response_control_refs(
    assessment: ResponseControlAssessment | dict[str, Any],
) -> dict[str, Any]:
    payload = (
        assessment.model_dump(mode="json")
        if isinstance(assessment, ResponseControlAssessment)
        else assessment
    )
    pool_selection = payload.get("domain_knowledge_package_selection") or {}
    runtime_environment_selection = payload.get("runtime_environment_selection") or {}
    technique_selection = payload.get("technique_selection") or {}
    return {
        "response_control_ref": response_control_artifact_ref(payload),
        "selected_domain_knowledge_package_refs": list(
            pool_selection.get("selected_package_refs") or []
        ),
        "selected_runtime_environment_refs": list(
            runtime_environment_selection.get("selected_runtime_environment_refs") or []
        ),
        "selected_technique_refs": list(
            technique_selection.get("selected_technique_refs") or []
        ),
        "selected_theory_refs": list(pool_selection.get("selected_theory_refs") or []),
    }


def evaluate_response_control(
    *,
    prompt: str | None = None,
    messages: list[dict[str, Any]] | None = None,
    context: dict[str, Any] | None = None,
    requested_agent_profile: str | None = None,
    active_agent_profile: str | None = None,
    minimum_agent_profile: str | None = None,
    catalog: ResponseControlCatalog | None = None,
) -> ResponseControlAssessment:
    """Evaluate the independent response-control choices for the current prompt."""

    ctx = context or {}
    text = (prompt or _latest_user_content(messages)).strip()
    lower = text.lower()
    loaded = catalog or load_response_control_catalog()
    selected_agent_profile, agent_profile_confidence, agent_profile_reason = _infer_agent_profile(
        lower=lower, catalog=loaded
    )
    explicit_agent_profile = _normalize_agent_profile(
        requested_agent_profile
        or ctx.get("agent_profile")
        or ctx.get("engagement_mode")
        or ("engineering" if ctx.get("strict_engineering") is True else None)
    )
    session_agent_profile = _normalize_agent_profile(
        active_agent_profile
        or ctx.get("active_agent_profile")
        or ctx.get("active_engagement_mode")
        or ctx.get("session_engagement_mode")
    )
    minimum = _normalize_agent_profile(minimum_agent_profile or ctx.get("minimum_agent_profile"))
    agent_profile_reasons = [agent_profile_reason]
    user_override = explicit_agent_profile is not None
    if explicit_agent_profile is not None:
        if explicit_agent_profile != selected_agent_profile:
            agent_profile_dissonance = AgentProfileDissonance(
                inferred_agent_profile=selected_agent_profile,
                suggested_agent_profile=selected_agent_profile,
                reason=(
                    f"Prompt evidence suggests {selected_agent_profile.value}, but explicit "
                    f"agent profile {explicit_agent_profile.value} remains authoritative."
                ),
            )
        else:
            agent_profile_dissonance = None
        selected_agent_profile = explicit_agent_profile
        agent_profile_confidence = 1.0
        agent_profile_reasons.append(f"explicit_agent_profile:{selected_agent_profile.value}")
    else:
        agent_profile_dissonance = None
        selected_agent_profile = session_agent_profile or minimum or selected_agent_profile
        if session_agent_profile is not None:
            agent_profile_reasons.append(f"session_agent_profile:{session_agent_profile.value}")
        if minimum is not None:
            agent_profile_reasons.append(f"minimum_agent_profile:{minimum.value}")

    selected_domain_knowledge_packages, package_reasons = _select_domain_knowledge_packages(
        lower=lower,
        selected_agent_profile=selected_agent_profile,
        catalog=loaded,
        context=ctx,
    )
    selected_theory_refs = _theory_refs_for_domain_knowledge_packages(
        selected_domain_knowledge_packages
    )
    selected_runtime_environments, runtime_environment_reasons = _select_runtime_environments(
        lower=lower,
        selected_domain_knowledge_packages=selected_domain_knowledge_packages,
        catalog=loaded,
        context=ctx,
    )
    selected_technique_refs = _technique_refs_for_runtime_environments(
        selected_runtime_environments
    )
    selected_package_refs = [
        _package_ref(package.domain_knowledge_package_id)
        for package in selected_domain_knowledge_packages
    ]
    selected_runtime_environment_refs = [
        _runtime_environment_ref(runtime_environment.runtime_environment_id)
        for runtime_environment in selected_runtime_environments
    ]
    selected_runtime_environment_refs_by_kind = {
        RuntimeEnvironmentKind.APPLICATION_RUNTIME: [
            _runtime_environment_ref(runtime_environment.runtime_environment_id)
            for runtime_environment in selected_runtime_environments
            if runtime_environment.runtime_environment_kind
            is RuntimeEnvironmentKind.APPLICATION_RUNTIME
        ],
        RuntimeEnvironmentKind.PACKAGE_RUNTIME: [
            _runtime_environment_ref(runtime_environment.runtime_environment_id)
            for runtime_environment in selected_runtime_environments
            if runtime_environment.runtime_environment_kind is RuntimeEnvironmentKind.PACKAGE_RUNTIME
        ],
        RuntimeEnvironmentKind.REFERENCE_RUNTIME: [
            _runtime_environment_ref(runtime_environment.runtime_environment_id)
            for runtime_environment in selected_runtime_environments
            if runtime_environment.runtime_environment_kind is RuntimeEnvironmentKind.REFERENCE_RUNTIME
        ],
    }
    assessment_id = uuid5(
        NAMESPACE_URL,
        "response-control-assessment:"
        + json.dumps(
            {
                "text": text,
                "agent_profile": selected_agent_profile.value,
                "domain_knowledge_packages": selected_package_refs,
                "runtime_environments": selected_runtime_environment_refs,
                "techniques": selected_technique_refs,
                "theory": selected_theory_refs,
            },
            sort_keys=True,
        ),
    )
    return ResponseControlAssessment(
        response_control_assessment_id=assessment_id,
        schema_version="1.0.0",
        agent_profile_selection=AgentProfileSelection(
            selected_agent_profile=selected_agent_profile,
            user_override=user_override,
            confidence=round(min(agent_profile_confidence, 1.0), 3),
            reasons=list(dict.fromkeys(agent_profile_reasons)),
            agent_profile_dissonance=agent_profile_dissonance,
        ),
        domain_knowledge_package_selection=DomainKnowledgePackageSelection(
            selected_package_refs=selected_package_refs,
            selected_theory_refs=selected_theory_refs,
            reasons=package_reasons,
        ),
        runtime_environment_selection=RuntimeEnvironmentSelection(
            selected_runtime_environment_refs_by_kind=selected_runtime_environment_refs_by_kind,
            selected_runtime_environment_refs=selected_runtime_environment_refs,
            reasons=runtime_environment_reasons,
        ),
        technique_selection=TechniqueSelection(
            selected_technique_refs=selected_technique_refs,
            derived_from_runtime_environment_refs=selected_runtime_environment_refs,
        ),
        assembly_order=list(ASSEMBLY_ORDER),
        created_at=datetime.now(UTC),
    )


def load_response_control_catalog(root: Path | None = None) -> ResponseControlCatalog:
    global _CATALOG_CACHE  # noqa: PLW0603 - intentional process-local cache
    base = root or _catalog_root()
    fingerprint = _catalog_fingerprint(base)
    if _CATALOG_CACHE and _CATALOG_CACHE[0] == fingerprint:
        return _CATALOG_CACHE[1]
    catalog = ResponseControlCatalog.load(base)
    _CATALOG_CACHE = (fingerprint, catalog)
    return catalog


def _catalog_root() -> Path:
    """Locate compiled routing JSON (``knowledge/response-control/*.json``)."""
    cwd = Path.cwd().resolve()
    for start in (cwd, *cwd.parents):
        for rel in ("xlotyl/knowledge/response-control", "knowledge/response-control"):
            candidate = start / rel
            if candidate.is_dir():
                return candidate
    here = Path(__file__).resolve()
    for path in [here, *here.parents]:
        candidate = path / "knowledge" / "response-control"
        if candidate.is_dir():
            return candidate
    raise RuntimeError("Could not locate knowledge/response-control")


def _catalog_fingerprint(root: Path) -> str:
    parts: list[str] = []
    for path in sorted(root.glob("*.json")):
        stat = path.stat()
        parts.append(f"{path.name}:{stat.st_mtime_ns}:{stat.st_size}")
    return "|".join(parts)


def _load_cards(path: Path, model: type[Any]) -> list[Any]:
    payload = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    if not isinstance(payload, list):
        raise ValueError(f"{path} must contain a JSON array")
    return [model.model_validate(item) for item in payload]


def _latest_user_content(messages: list[dict[str, Any]] | None) -> str:
    if not messages:
        return ""
    for message in reversed(messages):
        if message.get("role") == "user":
            return str(message.get("content") or "")
    return str(messages[-1].get("content") or "")


def _normalize_agent_profile(value: Any) -> AgentProfileKey | None:
    if value is None:
        return None
    normalized = str(value).strip().lower().replace("-", "_").replace("/", "_")
    if normalized in _AGENT_PROFILE_ALIASES:
        return _AGENT_PROFILE_ALIASES[normalized]
    try:
        return AgentProfileKey(normalized)
    except ValueError:
        return None


def _infer_agent_profile(
    *, lower: str, catalog: ResponseControlCatalog
) -> tuple[AgentProfileKey, float, str]:
    best: tuple[int, AgentProfileKey, str] | None = None
    for agent_profile_payload in catalog.agent_profiles.values():
        agent_profile_key = _normalize_agent_profile(
            agent_profile_payload.agent_profile_key
            or agent_profile_payload.agent_profile_id
        )
        if agent_profile_key is None:
            continue
        matched = [
            keyword
            for keyword in agent_profile_payload.keywords
            if _keyword_matches(keyword, lower)
        ]
        if not matched:
            continue
        score = len(matched)
        reason = f"agent_profile_catalog_keyword:{agent_profile_key.value}:{matched[0]}"
        candidate = (score, agent_profile_key, reason)
        if best is None or (candidate[0], candidate[1].value) > (
            best[0],
            best[1].value,
        ):
            best = candidate
    if best is not None:
        confidence = min(0.95, 0.55 + (0.1 * min(best[0], 4)))
        return best[1], confidence, best[2]

    if "query" in catalog.agent_profiles:
        return AgentProfileKey.QUERY, 0.5, "catalog_default:query"
    if "casual_chat" in catalog.agent_profiles:
        return AgentProfileKey.CASUAL_CHAT, 0.5, "catalog_default:casual_chat"
    return AgentProfileKey.QUERY, 0.45, "catalog_default:query_fallback"


def _select_domain_knowledge_packages(
    *,
    lower: str,
    selected_agent_profile: AgentProfileKey,
    catalog: ResponseControlCatalog,
    context: dict[str, Any],
) -> tuple[list[DomainKnowledgePackagePayload], list[str]]:
    explicit_package_refs = context.get("selected_domain_knowledge_package_refs")
    if isinstance(explicit_package_refs, list) and explicit_package_refs:
        selected = [
            pool
            for pool in catalog.domain_knowledge_packages.values()
            if _package_ref(pool.domain_knowledge_package_id) in explicit_package_refs
            or pool.domain_knowledge_package_id in explicit_package_refs
        ]
        if selected:
            return selected, ["explicit:selected_domain_knowledge_package_refs"]

    scored: list[tuple[int, DomainKnowledgePackagePayload, list[str]]] = []
    for pool in catalog.domain_knowledge_packages.values():
        matched = [
            keyword for keyword in pool.keywords if _keyword_matches(keyword, lower)
        ]
        package_reasons = [
            f"package_keyword:{pool.package_key}:{keyword}" for keyword in matched
        ]
        score = len(matched) * 2
        if matched and selected_agent_profile in pool.default_for_agent_profiles:
            score += 1
            package_reasons.append(
                f"agent_profile_default:{selected_agent_profile.value}:{pool.package_key}"
            )
        if score > 0:
            scored.append((score, pool, package_reasons))
    scored.sort(key=lambda item: (-item[0], item[1].package_key))
    selected = [pool for _score, pool, _reasons in scored[:4]]
    reasons = [
        reason for _score, _pool, pool_reasons in scored[:4] for reason in pool_reasons
    ]
    if not selected:
        # Fallback to defaults for the mode if no keyword matches
        selected = [
            pool
            for pool in catalog.domain_knowledge_packages.values()
            if selected_agent_profile in pool.default_for_agent_profiles
        ]
        if selected:
            reasons = [
                f"agent_profile_default:{selected_agent_profile.value}_core_packages"
            ]
    return selected, reasons or ["domain_knowledge_package_selection:no_package_required"]


def _select_runtime_environments(
    *,
    lower: str,
    selected_domain_knowledge_packages: list[DomainKnowledgePackagePayload],
    catalog: ResponseControlCatalog,
    context: dict[str, Any],
) -> tuple[list[RuntimeEnvironmentPayload], list[str]]:
    explicit_runtime_environment_refs = context.get("selected_runtime_environment_refs")
    if isinstance(explicit_runtime_environment_refs, list) and explicit_runtime_environment_refs:
        selected = [
            module
            for module in catalog.runtime_environments.values()
            if _runtime_environment_ref(module.runtime_environment_id)
            in explicit_runtime_environment_refs
            or module.runtime_environment_id in explicit_runtime_environment_refs
        ]
        if selected:
            return selected, ["explicit:selected_runtime_environment_refs"]

    selected_package_refs = {
        _package_ref(pool.domain_knowledge_package_id)
        for pool in selected_domain_knowledge_packages
    }
    scored: list[tuple[int, RuntimeEnvironmentPayload, list[str]]] = []
    for module in catalog.runtime_environments.values():
        matched = [
            keyword for keyword in module.keywords if _keyword_matches(keyword, lower)
        ]
        pool_fit = bool(selected_package_refs.intersection(module.package_refs))
        score = len(matched) * 2 + (1 if matched and pool_fit else 0)
        if score > 0:
            reasons = [
                f"runtime_environment_keyword:{module.runtime_environment_key}:{keyword}" for keyword in matched
            ]
            if pool_fit:
                reasons.append(f"runtime_environment_package_fit:{module.runtime_environment_key}")
            scored.append((score, module, reasons))
    scored.sort(key=lambda item: (-item[0], item[1].runtime_environment_key))
    selected = [module for _score, module, _reasons in scored[:6]]
    reasons = [
        reason
        for _score, _module, module_reasons in scored[:6]
        for reason in module_reasons
    ]
    if selected_domain_knowledge_packages and not selected:
        selected_ref_set = set()
        for pool in selected_domain_knowledge_packages:
            for ref in pool.runtime_environment_refs[:2]:
                selected_ref_set.add(ref)
                if len(selected_ref_set) >= 4:
                    break
            if len(selected_ref_set) >= 4:
                break
        selected = [
            module
            for module in catalog.runtime_environments.values()
            if _runtime_environment_ref(module.runtime_environment_id) in selected_ref_set
        ]
        reasons = ["domain_knowledge_package_default:first_ranked_runtime_environments"]
    return selected, reasons or ["runtime_environment_selection:no_runtime_environment_required"]


def _theory_refs_for_domain_knowledge_packages(
    packages: list[DomainKnowledgePackagePayload],
) -> list[str]:
    return list(dict.fromkeys(ref for package in packages for ref in package.theory_refs))


def _technique_refs_for_runtime_environments(
    runtime_environments: list[RuntimeEnvironmentPayload],
) -> list[str]:
    return list(
        dict.fromkeys(ref for runtime_environment in runtime_environments for ref in runtime_environment.technique_refs)
    )


def _keyword_matches(keyword: str, lower: str) -> bool:
    normalized = keyword.lower().strip()
    if not normalized:
        return False
    if " " in normalized:
        return normalized in lower
    return (
        re.search(rf"(?<![a-z0-9]){re.escape(normalized)}(?![a-z0-9])", lower)
        is not None
    )


def _package_ref(pool_id: str) -> str:
    return f"artifact://domain-knowledge-package/{pool_id}"


def _runtime_environment_ref(runtime_environment_id: str) -> str:
    return f"artifact://runtime-environment/{runtime_environment_id}"
```

"""
Load Draft 2020-12 schemas from the repo and validate instances.

For agents: uses canonical `$id` registry under `schemas/control-plane/v1/registry.json`.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

def _repo_root() -> Path:
    """Walk up from this file until `schemas/control-plane/v1` exists."""
    here = Path(__file__).resolve()
    for p in [here, *here.parents]:
        if (
            p
            / "services"
            / "response-control-framework"
            / "schemas"
            / "control-plane"
            / "v1"
            / "registry.json"
        ).exists():
            return p
    raise RuntimeError("Could not locate repo root (schemas/control-plane/v1 missing)")


def _load_registry_store() -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
    root = _repo_root()
    reg_path = (
        root
        / "services"
        / "response-control-framework"
        / "schemas"
        / "control-plane"
        / "v1"
        / "registry.json"
    )
    manifest = json.loads(reg_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
    store: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] = {}
    for entry in manifest.get("schemas", []):
        path = (
            root
            / "services"
            / "response-control-framework"
            / "schemas"
            / "control-plane"
            / "v1"
            / entry["path"]
        )
        data = json.loads(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
        sid = data.get("$id")
        if sid != entry["id"]:
            raise RuntimeError(f"Schema $id mismatch for {entry['path']}")
        store[sid] = data
    return store


_store: dict[str, dict[str, Any]] | None = None


def get_schema_store() -> dict[str, dict[str, Any]]:
    global _store  # noqa: PLW0603 — intentional module cache
    if _store is None:
        _store = _load_registry_store()
    return _store


def _validator_for(schema_id: str) -> Draft202012Validator:
    store = get_schema_store()
    if schema_id not in store:
        raise KeyError(f"Unknown schema id: {schema_id}")
    schema = store[schema_id]
    resolver = jsonschema.RefResolver(base_uri="", referrer=None, store=store)
    Draft202012Validator.check_schema(schema)
    return Draft202012Validator(schema, resolver=resolver)


def _schema_error(
    *,
    schema_id: str,
    contract_type: str,
    error: jsonschema.exceptions.ValidationError,
) -> ContractValidationError:
    path = (
        "/" + "/".join(str(p) for p in error.absolute_path)
        if error.absolute_path
        else "/"
    )
    return ContractValidationError(
        error_code="SCHEMA_VALIDATION_FAILED",
        contract_type=contract_type,
        schema_id=schema_id,
        details=[
            ContractErrorDetail(
                path=path, message=error.message, keyword=error.validator
            )
        ],
    )


def _model_error(
    *,
    schema_id: str,
    contract_type: str,
    error: ValueError,
) -> ContractValidationError:
    return ContractValidationError(
        error_code="SCHEMA_VALIDATION_FAILED",
        contract_type=contract_type,
        schema_id=schema_id,
        details=[
            ContractErrorDetail(path="/", message=str(error), keyword="model_validate")
        ],
    )


def validate_task_card_json(data: dict[str, Any]) -> TaskCard:
    """JSON Schema + Pydantic consumer conformance for task_card."""
    v = _validator_for(TASK_CARD_SCHEMA_ID)
    try:
        v.validate(data)
    except jsonschema.exceptions.ValidationError as e:
        path = (
            "/" + "/".join(str(p) for p in e.absolute_path) if e.absolute_path else "/"
        )
        raise ContractValidationError(
            error_code="SCHEMA_VALIDATION_FAILED",
            contract_type="TASK_CARD",
            schema_id=TASK_CARD_SCHEMA_ID,
            details=[
                ContractErrorDetail(path=path, message=e.message, keyword=e.validator)
            ],
        ) from e
    try:
        return TaskCard.model_validate(data)
    except ValueError as e:
        raise ContractValidationError(
            error_code="SCHEMA_VALIDATION_FAILED",
            contract_type="TASK_CARD",
            schema_id=TASK_CARD_SCHEMA_ID,
            details=[
                ContractErrorDetail(path="/", message=str(e), keyword="model_validate")
            ],
        ) from e


def validate_typed_artifact_json(data: dict[str, Any]) -> None:
    """Schema-only validation for typed artifact envelope (Pydantic optional follow-up)."""
    v = _validator_for(ARTIFACT_RECORD_SCHEMA_ID)
    try:
        v.validate(data)
    except jsonschema.exceptions.ValidationError as e:
        path = (
            "/" + "/".join(str(p) for p in e.absolute_path) if e.absolute_path else "/"
        )
        raise ContractValidationError(
            error_code="SCHEMA_VALIDATION_FAILED",
            contract_type="ARTIFACT_RECORD",
            schema_id=ARTIFACT_RECORD_SCHEMA_ID,
            details=[
                ContractErrorDetail(path=path, message=e.message, keyword=e.validator)
            ],
        ) from e

def validate_technique_card_json(data: dict[str, Any]) -> TechniqueCardPayload:
    v = _validator_for(TECHNIQUE_CARD_SCHEMA_ID)
    try:
        v.validate(data)
    except jsonschema.exceptions.ValidationError as e:
        raise _schema_error(
            schema_id=TECHNIQUE_CARD_SCHEMA_ID,
            contract_type="TECHNIQUE_CARD",
            error=e,
        ) from e
    try:
        return TechniqueCardPayload.model_validate(data)
    except ValueError as e:
        raise _model_error(
            schema_id=TECHNIQUE_CARD_SCHEMA_ID,

def validate_problem_brief_json(data: dict[str, Any]) -> ProblemBrief:
    """JSON Schema + Pydantic consumer conformance for problem_brief."""

    except jsonschema.exceptions.ValidationError as e:
        path = (
            "/" + "/".join(str(p) for p in e.absolute_path) if e.absolute_path else "/"
        )
        raise ContractValidationError(

            schema_id=PROBLEM_BRIEF_SCHEMA_ID,

                ContractErrorDetail(path=path, message=e.message, keyword=e.validator)
            ],
        ) from e
    try:
        return ProblemBrief.model_validate(data)
    except ValueError as e:
        raise ContractValidationError(
            error_code="SCHEMA_VALIDATION_FAILED",
            contract_type="PROBLEM_BRIEF",
            schema_id=PROBLEM_BRIEF_SCHEMA_ID,
            details=[
                ContractErrorDetail(path="/", message=str(e), keyword="model_validate")

### `services/response-control-framework/src/response_control_framework/wiki_fs.py`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 2031 bytes

```python
"""Shared repo-root and markdown (JSON front matter) helpers for orchestration wiki."""

from __future__ import annotations

import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any


def repo_root() -> Path:
    """
    Resolve the repository root that contains ``knowledge/wiki``.

    Prefer the process working directory (Docker ``WORKDIR /app`` with mounted
    ``knowledge/``). Also walks parents from this package for dev checkouts.
    """
    cwd = Path.cwd().resolve()
    for base in (cwd, cwd / "xlotyl"):
        if (base / "knowledge" / "wiki").is_dir():
            return base
    here = Path(__file__).resolve()
    for parent in [here, *here.parents]:
        if (parent / "knowledge" / "wiki").is_dir():
            return parent
    raise RuntimeError("Could not locate repo root (knowledge/wiki missing)")


def orchestration_wiki_root(base: Path | None = None) -> Path:
    """``knowledge/wiki/orchestration`` under ``base`` (default: :func:`repo_root`)."""
    return (base or repo_root()) / "knowledge" / "wiki" / "orchestration"


def projects_wiki_root(base: Path | None = None) -> Path:
    """``knowledge/wiki/projects`` under ``base`` (default: :func:`repo_root`)."""
    return (base or repo_root()) / "knowledge" / "wiki" / "projects"


def split_front_matter(raw: str, path: Path) -> tuple[dict[str, Any], str]:
    """
    Parse ``---`` JSON front matter and trailing markdown body.

    Raises
    ------
    ValueError
        If delimiters or JSON are invalid.
    """
    if not raw.startswith("---"):
        raise ValueError(f"{path}: must start with front matter delimiter ---")
    rest = raw[3:].lstrip("\n")
    marker = "\n---\n"
    idx = rest.find(marker)
    if idx == -1:
        raise ValueError(f"{path}: missing closing front matter delimiter")
    front = rest[:idx].strip()
    body = rest[idx + len(marker) :]
    parsed = json.loads(front)
    if not isinstance(parsed, dict):
        raise ValueError(f"{path}: front matter must be a JSON object")
    return parsed, body
```

---

### `services/response-control-framework/src/response_control_framework/wiki_proposals.py`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 9449 bytes

```python
"""Wiki proposal queue helpers for editorial governance."""

from __future__ import annotations

import json
import re
from datetime import UTC, datetime
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any
from uuid import UUID, uuid4

from .contracts import (
    WikiEditArchiveReason,
    WikiEditKind,
    WikiEditProposalPayload,
    WikiEditProposalStatus,
)
from .validation import validate_wiki_edit_proposal_json
from .wiki_fs import repo_root as _wiki_repo_root
from .wiki_fs import split_front_matter as _split_front_matter

CAUTION_TEXT = "unapproved source, proceed with caution"
EDITABLE_DRAFT_FIELDS = frozenset(
    {
        "title",
        "summary",
        "proposed_content",
        "proposed_patch",
        "rationale",
        "provenance_refs",
        "confidence",
    }
)
WIKI_SHARDS: dict[str, str] = {
    "agent-profiles": "agent_profile_id",
    "domain-knowledge-packages": "domain_knowledge_package_id",
    "runtime-environments": "runtime_environment_id",
    "techniques": "technique_card_id",
    "theory": "theory_card_id",
}


def queue_root() -> Path:
    root = _wiki_repo_root() / "knowledge" / "wiki" / "_proposals"
    root.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    return root


def _slugify(value: str) -> str:
    cleaned = re.sub(r"[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]+", "_", value.strip())
    return cleaned.strip("_") or "proposal"


def proposal_path(proposal_id: str | UUID) -> Path:
    return queue_root() / f"{proposal_id}.md"


def write_proposal_file(payload: WikiEditProposalPayload) -> Path:
    path = proposal_path(payload.wiki_edit_proposal_id)
    front = json.dumps(payload.model_dump(mode="json"), indent=2, sort_keys=True)
    content = f"---\n{front}\n---\n\n{payload.summary}\n"
    path.write_text(content, encoding="utf-8")
    return path


def load_proposal_file(path: Path) -> WikiEditProposalPayload:
    data, _body = _split_front_matter(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), path)
    return validate_wiki_edit_proposal_json(data)


def list_proposals(
    *, status: WikiEditProposalStatus | None = None
) -> list[WikiEditProposalPayload]:
    proposals: list[WikiEditProposalPayload] = []
    for path in sorted(queue_root().glob("*.md")):
        if path.name.lower() == "readme.md":
            continue
        proposal = load_proposal_file(path)
        if status is not None and proposal.status is not status:
            continue
        proposals.append(proposal)
    return proposals


def create_proposal(
    *,
    target_ref: str,
    target_path: str,
    title: str,
    summary: str,
    proposed_content: str,
    rationale: str,
    provenance_refs: list[str],
    created_by: str,
    edit_kind: WikiEditKind = WikiEditKind.UPDATE,
    confidence: float = 0.5,
    proposed_patch: str | None = None,
) -> WikiEditProposalPayload:
    now = datetime.now(UTC)
    payload = WikiEditProposalPayload(
        wiki_edit_proposal_id=uuid4(),
        target_ref=target_ref,
        target_path=target_path,
        edit_kind=edit_kind,
        status=WikiEditProposalStatus.PROPOSED,
        title=title,
        summary=summary,
        proposed_content=proposed_content,
        proposed_patch=proposed_patch,
        rationale=rationale,
        provenance_refs=provenance_refs,
        confidence=confidence,
        unapproved_source=True,
        caution=CAUTION_TEXT,
        created_by=created_by,
        created_at=now,
        updated_at=now,
    )
    write_proposal_file(payload)
    return payload


def update_proposal_status(
    *,
    proposal_id: str,
    status: WikiEditProposalStatus,
    approver: str | None = None,
    approval_notes: str | None = None,
    promotion_ref: str | None = None,
    archive_reason: WikiEditArchiveReason | None = None,
    archive_notes: str | None = None,
) -> WikiEditProposalPayload:
    path = proposal_path(proposal_id)
    proposal = load_proposal_file(path)
    now = datetime.now(UTC)
    updated = proposal.model_copy(
        update={
            "status": status,
            "approved_by": approver or proposal.approved_by,
            "approval_notes": (
                approval_notes
                if approval_notes is not None
                else proposal.approval_notes
            ),
            "approved_at": (
                now
                if status
                in {WikiEditProposalStatus.APPROVED, WikiEditProposalStatus.PROMOTED}
                else proposal.approved_at
            ),
            "promoted_at": (
                now
                if status is WikiEditProposalStatus.PROMOTED
                else proposal.promoted_at
            ),
            "promotion_ref": (
                promotion_ref if promotion_ref is not None else proposal.promotion_ref
            ),
            "archived_at": (
                now if status is WikiEditProposalStatus.ARCHIVED else proposal.archived_at
            ),
            "archived_by": (
                approver if status is WikiEditProposalStatus.ARCHIVED else proposal.archived_by
            ),
            "archive_reason": (
                archive_reason
                if status is WikiEditProposalStatus.ARCHIVED
                else proposal.archive_reason
            ),
            "archive_notes": (
                archive_notes
                if status is WikiEditProposalStatus.ARCHIVED
                else proposal.archive_notes
            ),
            "updated_at": now,
        }
    )
    write_proposal_file(updated)
    return updated


def update_proposal_draft(
    *,
    proposal_id: str,
    updates: dict[str, Any],
) -> WikiEditProposalPayload:
    path = proposal_path(proposal_id)
    proposal = load_proposal_file(path)
    if proposal.status is not WikiEditProposalStatus.PROPOSED:
        raise ValueError("only PROPOSED proposals can be edited")
    normalized = {k: v for k, v in updates.items() if k in EDITABLE_DRAFT_FIELDS}
    if not normalized:
        raise ValueError("no editable draft fields supplied")
    merged = proposal.model_dump(mode="json")
    merged.update(normalized)
    merged["updated_at"] = datetime.now(UTC).isoformat()
    updated = validate_wiki_edit_proposal_json(merged)
    write_proposal_file(updated)
    return updated


def _load_orchestration_cards() -> list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any], str]]:
    repo = _wiki_repo_root()
    cards: list[tuple[str, dict[str, Any], str]] = []
    for shard, id_field in WIKI_SHARDS.items():
        for path in sorted(
            (repo / "knowledge" / "wiki" / "orchestration" / shard).glob("*.md")
        ):
            front, body = _split_front_matter(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"), path)
            if id_field not in front:
                continue
            cards.append((str(path), front, body.strip()))
    return cards


def _ref_for_card(front: dict[str, Any]) -> str | None:
    if "agent_profile_id" in front:
        return f"artifact://agent-profile/{front['agent_profile_id']}"
    if "domain_knowledge_package_id" in front:
        return f"artifact://domain-knowledge-package/{front['domain_knowledge_package_id']}"
    if "runtime_environment_id" in front:
        return f"artifact://runtime-environment/{front['runtime_environment_id']}"
    if "technique_card_id" in front:
        return f"artifact://technique-card/{front['technique_card_id']}"
    if "theory_card_id" in front:
        return f"artifact://theory-card/{front['theory_card_id']}"
    return None


def wiki_edit_proposal_refs_for_selected(selected_refs: list[str]) -> list[str]:
    """
    Return stable artifact refs for PROPOSED wiki edits whose ``target_ref`` is
    among ``selected_refs`` (same matching rules as :func:`resolve_wiki_overlay_context`).
    """
    refs = {str(ref).strip() for ref in selected_refs if str(ref).strip()}
    if not refs:
        return []
    out: list[str] = []
    for proposal in list_proposals(status=WikiEditProposalStatus.PROPOSED):
        if proposal.target_ref in refs:
            out.append(f"artifact://wiki_edit_proposal/{proposal.wiki_edit_proposal_id}")
    return sorted(out)


def resolve_wiki_overlay_context(selected_refs: list[str]) -> str:
    refs = {str(ref).strip() for ref in selected_refs if str(ref).strip()}
    if not refs:
        return ""
    approved_chunks: list[str] = []
    for _path, front, body in _load_orchestration_cards():
        ref = _ref_for_card(front)
        if not ref or ref not in refs:
            continue
        title = str(front.get("label") or front.get("title") or ref)
        snippet = body or str(front.get("summary") or "")
        approved_chunks.append(f"- {title} ({ref})\n  {snippet}")

    proposal_chunks: list[str] = []
    for proposal in list_proposals(status=WikiEditProposalStatus.PROPOSED):
        if proposal.target_ref not in refs:
            continue
        proposal_chunks.append(
            f"- {proposal.title} ({proposal.target_ref})\n"
            f"  {CAUTION_TEXT.upper()}\n"
            f"  Summary: {proposal.summary}\n"
            f"  Proposed content: {proposal.proposed_content}"
        )

    if not approved_chunks and not proposal_chunks:
        return ""
    sections: list[str] = []
    if approved_chunks:
        sections.append("Approved wiki context:\n" + "\n".join(approved_chunks))
    if proposal_chunks:
        sections.append(
            "Unapproved wiki overlays (proceed with caution):\n"
            + "\n".join(proposal_chunks)
        )
    return "\n\n".join(sections)
```

### `services/response-control-framework/src/response_control_framework/wiki_public.py`

- repo: `HHPE-HRG/xlotyl`
- size: 8755 bytes

```python
"""Orchestration and projects wiki readers (markdown + JSON front matter)."""

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass
import json
from pathlib import Path
from typing import Any

from .wiki_fs import orchestration_wiki_root, projects_wiki_root, split_front_matter


class WikiPathError(ValueError):
    """Invalid path within wiki roots."""


@dataclass
class WikiPageRecord:
    """Single wiki page: relative path, display title, markdown body (after front matter)."""

    path: str
    title: str
    body: str


def format_wiki_page_for_overlay(page: WikiPageRecord) -> str:
    """Format a wiki page for UI overlay display."""
    return f"# {page.title}\n\n{page.body}"


def _safe_rel_under(root: Path, raw: str) -> Path:
    """Resolve ``raw`` as a path under ``root``; reject traversal."""
    p = (raw or "").strip().replace("\\", "/").lstrip("/")
    if not p or ".." in p.split("/"):
        raise WikiPathError("invalid wiki path")
    candidate = (root / p).resolve()
    root_r = root.resolve()
    try:
        candidate.relative_to(root_r)
    except ValueError as exc:
        raise WikiPathError("path escapes wiki root") from exc
    return candidate


def normalize_orchestration_relative_path(raw: str) -> str:
    """Normalize a relative path under ``knowledge/wiki/orchestration``."""
    p = (raw or "").strip().replace("\\", "/").lstrip("/")
    if ".." in p.split("/"):
        raise WikiPathError("path traversal not allowed")
    return p


def normalize_projects_relative_path(raw: str) -> str:
    """Normalize a relative path under ``knowledge/wiki/projects``."""
    return normalize_orchestration_relative_path(raw)


def _title_from_front(front: dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    return str(front.get("label") or front.get("title") or front.get("summary") or "untitled")


def _render_page(front_matter: dict[str, Any], body: str) -> str:
    front = json.dumps(front_matter, indent=2, sort_keys=True)
    normalized_body = body.rstrip()
    return f"---\n{front}\n---\n{normalized_body}\n"


def get_orchestration_wiki_page(path: str, *, base: Path | None = None) -> WikiPageRecord:
    """Load one orchestration shard page by path relative to the orchestration root."""
    rel = normalize_orchestration_relative_path(path)
    root = orchestration_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"orchestration wiki page not found: {rel}")
    raw = file_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    front, body = split_front_matter(raw, file_path)
    title = _title_from_front(front)
    return WikiPageRecord(path=rel, title=title, body=body.strip())


def get_projects_wiki_page(path: str, *, base: Path | None = None) -> WikiPageRecord:
    """Load one projects wiki page by path relative to the projects root."""
    rel = normalize_projects_relative_path(path)
    root = projects_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"projects wiki page not found: {rel}")
    raw = file_path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
    front, body = split_front_matter(raw, file_path)
    title = _title_from_front(front)
    return WikiPageRecord(path=rel, title=title, body=body.strip())


def create_orchestration_wiki_page(
    path: str,
    front_matter: dict[str, Any],
    body: str,
    *,
    base: Path | None = None,
) -> WikiPageRecord:
    """Create one orchestration wiki page under the canonical root."""
    rel = normalize_orchestration_relative_path(path)
    root = orchestration_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if file_path.exists():
        raise FileExistsError(f"orchestration wiki page already exists: {rel}")
    file_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    file_path.write_text(_render_page(front_matter, body), encoding="utf-8")
    return get_orchestration_wiki_page(rel, base=base)


def update_orchestration_wiki_page(
    path: str,
    front_matter: dict[str, Any],
    body: str,
    *,
    base: Path | None = None,
) -> WikiPageRecord:
    """Update one orchestration wiki page under the canonical root."""
    rel = normalize_orchestration_relative_path(path)
    root = orchestration_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"orchestration wiki page not found: {rel}")
    file_path.write_text(_render_page(front_matter, body), encoding="utf-8")
    return get_orchestration_wiki_page(rel, base=base)


def delete_orchestration_wiki_page(path: str, *, base: Path | None = None) -> None:
    """Delete one orchestration wiki page under the canonical root."""
    rel = normalize_orchestration_relative_path(path)
    root = orchestration_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"orchestration wiki page not found: {rel}")
    file_path.unlink()


def create_projects_wiki_page(
    path: str,
    front_matter: dict[str, Any],
    body: str,
    *,
    base: Path | None = None,
) -> WikiPageRecord:
    """Create one projects wiki page under the canonical root."""
    rel = normalize_projects_relative_path(path)
    root = projects_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if file_path.exists():
        raise FileExistsError(f"projects wiki page already exists: {rel}")
    file_path.parent.mkdir(parents=True, exist_ok=True)
    file_path.write_text(_render_page(front_matter, body), encoding="utf-8")
    return get_projects_wiki_page(rel, base=base)


def update_projects_wiki_page(
    path: str,
    front_matter: dict[str, Any],
    body: str,
    *,
    base: Path | None = None,
) -> WikiPageRecord:
    """Update one projects wiki page under the canonical root."""
    rel = normalize_projects_relative_path(path)
    root = projects_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"projects wiki page not found: {rel}")
    file_path.write_text(_render_page(front_matter, body), encoding="utf-8")
    return get_projects_wiki_page(rel, base=base)


def delete_projects_wiki_page(path: str, *, base: Path | None = None) -> None:
    """Delete one projects wiki page under the canonical root."""
    rel = normalize_projects_relative_path(path)
    root = projects_wiki_root(base)
    file_path = _safe_rel_under(root, rel)
    if not file_path.is_file():
        raise FileNotFoundError(f"projects wiki page not found: {rel}")
    file_path.unlink()


def list_orchestration_wiki_pages(*, base: Path | None = None) -> list[str]:
    """List relative paths to all ``*.md`` files under orchestration (excluding README)."""
    root = orchestration_wiki_root(base)
    if not root.is_dir():
        return []
    out: list[str] = []
    for path in sorted(root.rglob("*.md")):
        if path.name.lower() == "readme.md":
            continue
        rel = path.relative_to(root.resolve())
        out.append(str(rel).replace("\\", "/"))
    return out


def list_projects_wiki_pages(*, base: Path | None = None) -> list[str]:
    """List relative paths to all ``*.md`` under projects wiki."""
    root = projects_wiki_root(base)
    if not root.is_dir():
        return []
    out: list[str] = []
    for path in sorted(root.rglob("*.md")):
        if path.name.lower() == "readme.md":
            continue
        rel = path.relative_to(root.resolve())
        out.append(str(rel).replace("\\", "/"))
    return out


def search_orchestration_wiki(query: str, *, base: Path | None = None) -> list[WikiPageRecord]:
    """
    Case-insensitive substring search over title (front matter) and body text.

    Parameters
    ----------
    query
        Non-empty search string (whitespace stripped).

    Returns
    -------
    list[WikiPageRecord]
        Pages that match, sorted by relative path.
    """
    q = (query or "").strip().lower()
    if not q:
        return []
    root = orchestration_wiki_root(base)
    if not root.is_dir():
        return []
    hits: list[WikiPageRecord] = []
    for path in sorted(root.rglob("*.md")):
        if path.name.lower() == "readme.md":
            continue
        try:
            raw = path.read_text(encoding="utf-8")
            front, body = split_front_matter(raw, path)
        except (OSError, ValueError, UnicodeDecodeError):
            continue
        title = _title_from_front(front)
        blob = f"{title}\n{body}".lower()
        if q not in blob:
            continue
        rel = str(path.relative_to(root.resolve())).replace("\\", "/")
        hits.append(WikiPageRecord(path=rel, title=title, body=body.strip()))
    return hits
```
